### ๐๏ธ ุฌุฏุงูู ุฏุชุงุจุณ (ุณุงุฎุช ฺฉุฌุง ุฏุฑ `class-novel-core.php` โ activation hook)

```sql
-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑ: ุฑุฃ ุฏุฏฺฏุงู (ูุงฺฉ/ุฏุณูุงฺฉ) โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}comment_votes (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    comment_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    vote TINYINT NOT NULL,                -- 1=like, -1=dislike
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_vote (comment_id, user_id),
    INDEX idx_comment (comment_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฒ: ุฑโุงฺฉุดู ุงููุฌ ุฏุฏฺฏุงู โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}comment_reactions (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    comment_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    reaction VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,        -- love, shocked, sad, angry, fire
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_reaction (comment_id, user_id),
    INDEX idx_comment_reaction (comment_id, reaction)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ณ: ุฑุฃ ููุฏ/ุบุฑููุฏ ููุฏ โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}review_helpfulness (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    comment_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    helpful TINYINT NOT NULL,             -- 1=ููุฏ, -1=ุบุฑููุฏ
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_helpful (comment_id, user_id),
    INDEX idx_comment (comment_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ด: ุฑุฃ ูุงฺฉ/ุฏุณูุงฺฉ ูุณูุช โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}chapter_votes (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    chapter_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    vote TINYINT NOT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_vote (chapter_id, user_id),
    INDEX idx_chapter (chapter_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ต: ฺฏุฒุงุฑุดโูุง (ฺฉูพุงุฑฺู) โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}reports (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    reporter_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    reported_type ENUM('chapter','comment','user','novel') NOT NULL,
    reported_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    reason VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT NULL,
    status ENUM('pending','reviewed','resolved','rejected') DEFAULT 'pending',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    reviewed_at DATETIME NULL,
    reviewed_by BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL,
    admin_note TEXT NULL,
    INDEX idx_status (status),
    INDEX idx_type_id (reported_type, reported_id),
    UNIQUE KEY unique_report (reporter_id, reported_type, reported_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ถ: ุงุนูุงูโูุง โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}notifications (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    title VARCHAR(300) NOT NULL,
    message TEXT NULL,
    link VARCHAR(500) NULL,
    image_url VARCHAR(500) NULL,
    is_read TINYINT DEFAULT 0,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_user_read (user_id, is_read),
    INDEX idx_created (created_at)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ท: ูุงูู ฺฉุงุฑุจุฑ (ููุณูุฏู) โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}user_follows (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    follower_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    following_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_follow (follower_id, following_id),
    INDEX idx_following (following_id),
    INDEX idx_follower (follower_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ธ: ุฏูุจุงู ฺฉุฑุฏู ุฑูุงู โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}novel_follows (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    notify_new_chapter TINYINT DEFAULT 1,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_follow (user_id, novel_id),
    INDEX idx_novel (novel_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู น: ฺฉุชุงุจุฎุงูู ุดุฎุต โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}user_library (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    list_type ENUM('reading','plan_to_read','completed','dropped','on_hold') NOT NULL,
    last_chapter_id BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    progress_percent DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    added_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_entry (user_id, novel_id),
    INDEX idx_user_list (user_id, list_type)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑฐ: ุชุงุฑุฎฺู ูุทุงูุนู โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}reading_history (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    chapter_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    scroll_position FLOAT DEFAULT 0,
    read_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_read (user_id, chapter_id),
    INDEX idx_user_novel (user_id, novel_id),
    INDEX idx_read_at (read_at)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑฑ: ุณฺฉูโูุง โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}user_coins (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    amount INT NOT NULL,                  -- ูุซุจุช=ุดุงุฑฺุ ููู=ูุตุฑู
    balance_after INT NOT NULL,
    type ENUM('purchase','subscription_bonus','spend','refund','admin_grant','expired') NOT NULL,
    description VARCHAR(300) NULL,
    related_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL,      -- chapter_id ุง order_id
    expires_at DATETIME NULL,             -- ุชุงุฑุฎ ุงููุถุง (null=ุจุฏูู ุงููุถุง)
    is_expired TINYINT DEFAULT 0,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_user (user_id),
    INDEX idx_expires (expires_at, is_expired),
    INDEX idx_type (type)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑฒ: ุฎุฑุฏ ูุณูุช ุจุง ุณฺฉู โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}chapter_purchases (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    chapter_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    coins_spent INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    purchased_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_purchase (user_id, chapter_id),
    INDEX idx_novel (novel_id),
    INDEX idx_user (user_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑณ: ุฏุฑุขูุฏ ููุณูุฏู โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}author_earnings (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    author_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    chapter_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    buyer_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    coins_earned INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    real_value DECIMAL(12,0) DEFAULT 0,   -- ูุนุงุฏู ุฑุงู
    commission_rate DECIMAL(3,2) DEFAULT 0.70,  -- ทฐูช ุณูู ููุณูุฏู
    status ENUM('pending','paid','cancelled') DEFAULT 'pending',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_author (author_id),
    INDEX idx_status (status),
    INDEX idx_novel (novel_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑด: ูุงุฑุฒโูุง ููุณูุฏู โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}author_payouts (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    author_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    amount DECIMAL(12,0) NOT NULL,
    payment_method VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    payment_details TEXT NULL,
    transaction_id VARCHAR(100) NULL,
    status ENUM('pending','processing','completed','failed') DEFAULT 'pending',
    requested_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    processed_at DATETIME NULL,
    processed_by BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL,
    note TEXT NULL,
    INDEX idx_author (author_id),
    INDEX idx_status (status)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑต: ูุธุฑุณูุฌ โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}polls (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(300) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT NULL,
    type ENUM('single','multiple') DEFAULT 'single',
    status ENUM('active','closed','draft') DEFAULT 'active',
    start_date DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    end_date DATETIME NULL,
    created_by BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
) {$charset_collate};

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}poll_options (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    poll_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    option_text VARCHAR(300) NOT NULL,
    votes_count INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    INDEX idx_poll (poll_id)
) {$charset_collate};

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}poll_votes (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    poll_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    option_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_vote (poll_id, user_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑถ: ุฏุณุชุงูุฑุฏูุง โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}user_achievements (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    achievement_slug VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    earned_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_achievement (user_id, achievement_slug),
    INDEX idx_user (user_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑท: ูุธุฑุงุช ุฏุฑุจุงุฑู ููุณูุฏู โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}author_reviews (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    author_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    reviewer_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    rating TINYINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,    -- ฑ ุชุง ต
    parent_id BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    likes_count INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    dislikes_count INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'approved',
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_author (author_id),
    INDEX idx_parent (parent_id)
) {$charset_collate};

-- โโโ ุฌุฏูู ฑธ: ุจุงุฒุฏุฏ (ุงุฑุชูุงุงูุชู) โโโ
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}novel_views (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    post_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    ip_address VARCHAR(45) NULL,
    view_date DATE NOT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE KEY unique_view (post_id, user_id, ip_address, view_date),
    INDEX idx_post_date (post_id, view_date),
    INDEX idx_date (view_date)
) {$charset_collate};
```

**ูฺฉุงุช ุณุงุฎุช ุฌุฏุงูู:**
- `dbDelta()` ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ุดูุฏ

## โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ
## ูุงุฒ ฑต: PWA + ุงูพูฺฉุดู ููุจุงู + REST API
## โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ

### ฑต.ฑ PWA (Progressive Web App)

```
ูุงูโูุง ุฌุฏุฏ:
  - manifest.json (ุฑุดู ุณุงุช)
  - sw.js (Service Worker - ุฑุดู ุณุงุช)
  - inc/class-novel-pwa.php

โโโ manifest.json โโโ
{
  "name": "[ูุงู ุณุงุช]",
  "short_name": "[ูุงู ฺฉูุชุงู]",
  "description": "ุณุงุช ุฑูุงู ุขููุงู ูุงุฑุณ",
  "start_url": "/",
  "display": "standalone",
  "orientation": "portrait",
  "background_color": "#1A1A2E",
  "theme_color": "#6C5CE7",
  "lang": "fa",
  "dir": "rtl",
  "icons": [
    {"src": "/icon-72.png", "sizes": "72x72", "type": "image/png"},
    {"src": "/icon-96.png", "sizes": "96x96", "type": "image/png"},
    {"src": "/icon-128.png", "sizes": "128x128", "type": "image/png"},
    {"src": "/icon-144.png", "sizes": "144x144", "type": "image/png"},
    {"src": "/icon-152.png", "sizes": "152x152", "type": "image/png"},
    {"src": "/icon-192.png", "sizes": "192x192", "type": "image/png"},
    {"src": "/icon-384.png", "sizes": "384x384", "type": "image/png"},
    {"src": "/icon-512.png", "sizes": "512x512", "type": "image/png"}
  ],
  "categories": ["books", "entertainment"],
  "screenshots": [
    {"src": "/screenshot-1.png", "sizes": "1080x1920", "type": "image/png"}
  ]
}

โโโ Service Worker (sw.js) โโโ

  ุงุณุชุฑุงุชฺโูุง:
  - Shell (CSS/JS/fonts): Cache First
  - API (AJAX): Network First โ fallback cache
  - Images: Cache First with expiry (30 ุฑูุฒ)
  - Pages: Network First โ fallback cache โ fallback offline page
  - Chapter content: Cache after read (ุฎูุงููุฏู ุขููุงู ุจุฎูุงูุฏ)

  const CACHE_NAME = 'novel-v2.0.0';
  const OFFLINE_URL = '/offline/';
  
  // Install: cache shell
  self.addEventListener('install', event => {
    event.waitUntil(
      caches.open(CACHE_NAME).then(cache => {
        return cache.addAll([
          '/',
          '/assets/css/main.css',
          '/assets/js/main.js',
          '/offline/',
          // fonts, icons
        ]);
      })
    );
  });
  
  // Fetch: strategy routing
  self.addEventListener('fetch', event => {
    const url = new URL(event.request.url);
    
    // CSS/JS/fonts โ Cache First
    if (url.pathname.match(/\.(css|js|woff2|svg)$/)) {
      event.respondWith(cacheFirst(event.request));
    }
    // Images โ Cache First + expiry
    else if (url.pathname.match(/\.(png|jpg|gif|webp)$/)) {
      event.respondWith(cacheFirst(event.request));
    }
    // API โ Network First
    else if (url.pathname.includes('admin-ajax.php')) {
      event.respondWith(networkFirst(event.request));
    }
    // Pages โ Network First โ offline
    else {
      event.respondWith(networkFirstWithOffline(event.request));
    }
  });

  // Background sync ุจุฑุง ุงุฑุณุงู ุฏุฏฺฏุงู ุขููุงู
  self.addEventListener('sync', event => {
    if (event.tag === 'novel-comment-sync') {
      event.waitUntil(syncComments());
    }
  });

  // Push notifications
  self.addEventListener('push', event => {
    const data = event.data.json();
    self.registration.showNotification(data.title, {
      body: data.message,
      icon: '/icon-192.png',
      badge: '/badge-72.png',
      data: { url: data.link },
      dir: 'rtl',
      lang: 'fa',
    });
  });
```

```
  // src/api/client.js
  import axios from 'axios';
  import AsyncStorage from '@react-native-async-storage/async-storage';

  const API_BASE = 'https://YOUR-SITE.com/wp-json/novel/v1';

  const client = axios.create({
    baseURL: API_BASE,
    timeout: 15000,
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
  });

  // Interceptor: ุงุถุงูู ฺฉุฑุฏู JWT token
  client.interceptors.request.use(async (config) => {
    const token = await AsyncStorage.getItem('auth_token');
    if (token) config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
    return config;
  });

  // Interceptor: handle 401
  client.interceptors.response.use(
    (response) => response,
    async (error) => {
      if (error.response?.status === 401) {
        await AsyncStorage.removeItem('auth_token');
        // Navigate to login
      }
      return Promise.reject(error);
    }
  );

  export default client;
```

### ฑถ.ฒ ุงููุช

```

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}quizzes (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(300) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT NULL,
    novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL,         -- ูุฎุชุต ฺฉ ุฑูุงู (NULL=ุนููู)
    chapter_range_start INT UNSIGNED NULL,  -- ุงุฒ ูุณูุช X
    chapter_range_end INT UNSIGNED NULL,    -- ุชุง ูุณูุช Y
    difficulty ENUM('easy','medium','hard','mixed') DEFAULT 'medium',
    time_per_question INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 30,  -- ุซุงูู
    total_questions INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 10,
    reward_coins INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 5,    -- ุฌุงุฒู ุณฺฉู ุจุฑูุฏู
    reward_coins_participation INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 1,  -- ุณฺฉู ุดุฑฺฉุช
    max_participants INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,  -- 0=ูุงูุญุฏูุฏ
    quiz_type ENUM('daily','weekly','event','custom') DEFAULT 'custom',
    start_time DATETIME NULL,               -- ุฒูุงู ุดุฑูุน (NULL=ูุฑ ููุช)
    end_time DATETIME NULL,
    is_repeatable TINYINT DEFAULT 0,        -- ุขุง ุจุงุฑูุง ุดุฑฺฉุช ฺฉูุฏ
    status ENUM('draft','active','closed','archived') DEFAULT 'draft',
    created_by BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_novel (novel_id),
    INDEX idx_status (status),
    INDEX idx_type (quiz_type),
    INDEX idx_start (start_time)
) {$charset_collate};

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}quiz_questions (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    quiz_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    question_text TEXT NOT NULL,
    question_type ENUM('multiple','true_false','fill_blank') DEFAULT 'multiple',
    option_a VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    option_b VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    option_c VARCHAR(500) NULL,            -- NULL ุจุฑุง true/false
    option_d VARCHAR(500) NULL,
    correct_answer ENUM('a','b','c','d') NOT NULL,
    explanation TEXT NULL,                  -- ุชูุถุญ ูพุงุณุฎ ุตุญุญ
    chapter_reference INT UNSIGNED NULL,    -- ูุฑุฌุน: ูุณูุช ฺูุฏ
    difficulty ENUM('easy','medium','hard') DEFAULT 'medium',
    points INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 10,         -- ุงูุชุงุฒ ุงู ุณูุงู
    sort_order INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    INDEX idx_quiz (quiz_id)
) {$charset_collate};

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}quiz_attempts (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    quiz_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    score INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    total_points INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    correct_count INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    wrong_count INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    time_spent INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,      -- ุซุงูู
    coins_earned INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
    started_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    completed_at DATETIME NULL,
    status ENUM('in_progress','completed','abandoned') DEFAULT 'in_progress',
    INDEX idx_quiz_user (quiz_id, user_id),
    INDEX idx_user (user_id),
    INDEX idx_score (quiz_id, score DESC)
) {$charset_collate};

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}quiz_answers (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    attempt_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    question_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
    user_answer ENUM('a','b','c','d') NULL,
    is_correct TINYINT DEFAULT 0,
    time_spent INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,      -- ุซุงูู ุจุฑุง ุงู ุณูุงู
    answered_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,

) {$charset_collate};
```

```
      error_log($log);
    }
  }

  ุณุทูุญ: info, warning, error, critical
  ุงุณุชูุงุฏู: novel_log('ุฎุทุง ุฏุฑ ุซุจุช ุฑุฃ', 'error', ['user' => $id])
```

```
  CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}discussion_messages (
      id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
      room_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      message TEXT NOT NULL,
      message_type ENUM('text','sticker','gif','system') DEFAULT 'text',
      is_spoiler TINYINT DEFAULT 0,
      reply_to BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL,
      created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
      expires_at DATETIME NOT NULL,
      INDEX idx_room (room_id, created_at),
      INDEX idx_expires (expires_at)
  ) {$charset_collate};

  CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}discussion_rooms (
      id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
      novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      is_active TINYINT DEFAULT 1,
      online_count INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
      total_messages BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
      created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
      UNIQUE KEY unique_novel (novel_id)
  ) {$charset_collate};

  CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}discussion_mutes (
      id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
      room_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      muted_by BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      reason VARCHAR(200) NULL,
      muted_until DATETIME NOT NULL,
      created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
      UNIQUE KEY unique_mute (room_id, user_id)
  ) {$charset_collate};
```

```
  CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}discussion_messages (
      id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
      room_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      message TEXT NOT NULL,
      message_type ENUM('text','sticker','gif','system') DEFAULT 'text',
      is_spoiler TINYINT DEFAULT 0,
      reply_to BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL,
      created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
      expires_at DATETIME NOT NULL,
      INDEX idx_room (room_id, created_at),
      INDEX idx_expires (expires_at)
  ) {$charset_collate};

  CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}discussion_rooms (
      id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
      novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      is_active TINYINT DEFAULT 1,
      online_count INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
      total_messages BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
      created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
      UNIQUE KEY unique_novel (novel_id)
  ) {$charset_collate};

  CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}discussion_mutes (
      id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
      room_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      muted_by BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
      reason VARCHAR(200) NULL,
      muted_until DATETIME NOT NULL,
      created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
      UNIQUE KEY unique_mute (room_id, user_id)
  ) {$charset_collate};
```

```
CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}discussion_messages (
  id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  message TEXT NOT NULL,
  message_type ENUM('text','sticker','gif','system') DEFAULT 'text',
  is_spoiler TINYINT DEFAULT 0,
  reply_to BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  expires_at DATETIME NOT NULL,
  INDEX idx_room (room_id, created_at),
  INDEX idx_expires (expires_at)
) {$charset_collate};

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}discussion_rooms (
  id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
  novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  is_active TINYINT DEFAULT 1,
  online_count INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
  total_messages BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  UNIQUE KEY unique_novel (novel_id)
) {$charset_collate};

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}discussion_mutes (
  id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  muted_by BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  reason VARCHAR(200) NULL,
  muted_until DATETIME NOT NULL,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  UNIQUE KEY unique_mute (room_id, user_id)
) {$charset_collate};

// JS ุณูุช ฺฉูุงูุช:
function pollMessages(roomId, lastId) {
  fetch(NovelAjax.url, {
    method: 'POST',
    body: new URLSearchParams({
      action: 'novel_get_messages',
      nonce: NovelAjax.nonce,
      room_id: roomId,
      last_id: lastId,
      timeout: 25  // ุซุงูู ุงูุชุธุงุฑ ุณุฑูุฑ
    })
  })
  .then(r => r.json())
  .then(data => {
    if (data.messages.length > 0) {
      appendMessages(data.messages);
      lastId = data.last_id;
    }
    // ููุฑุงู ุฏูุจุงุฑู poll ฺฉู
    pollMessages(roomId, lastId);
  })
  .catch(() => {
    // ุฎุทุง: ต ุซุงูู ุตุจุฑ ฺฉู
    setTimeout(() => pollMessages(roomId, lastId), 5000);
  });
}

// PHP ุณูุช ุณุฑูุฑ:
function get_messages() {
  $room_id = absint($_POST['room_id']);
  $last_id = absint($_POST['last_id']);
  $timeout = min(absint($_POST['timeout']), 30);
  
  $start = time();
  while (time() - $start < $timeout) {
    $messages = $wpdb->get_results(
      $wpdb->prepare(
        "SELECT * FROM {$prefix}discussion_messages 
         WHERE room_id = %d AND id > %d 
         ORDER BY id ASC LIMIT 50",
        $room_id, $last_id
      )
    );
    
    if (!empty($messages)) {
      wp_send_json_success([
        'messages' => $messages,
        'last_id' => end($messages)->id
      ]);
    }
    
    // ฑ ุซุงูู ุตุจุฑ ูุจู ฺฺฉ ุจุนุฏ
    sleep(1);
  }
  
  // timeout: ุฎุงู ุจุฑฺฏุฑุฏูู
  wp_send_json_success(['messages' => [], 'last_id' => $last_id]);
}

โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}story_predictions (
  id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
  chapter_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  novel_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  author_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  question TEXT NOT NULL,
  options JSON NOT NULL,
  correct_option TINYINT NULL,
  status ENUM('active','resolved','expired') DEFAULT 'active',
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  resolved_at DATETIME NULL,
  INDEX idx_chapter (chapter_id),
  INDEX idx_novel (novel_id),
  INDEX idx_status (status)
) {$charset_collate};

CREATE TABLE {$wpdb->prefix}prediction_votes (
  id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
  prediction_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  selected_option TINYINT NOT NULL,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  UNIQUE KEY unique_vote (prediction_id, user_id),
  INDEX idx_prediction (prediction_id)
) {$charset_collate};
```
